/* The Great Computer Language Shootout
   http://shootout.alioth.debian.org/
   contributed by Isaac Gouy */

function fannkuch(n) {
   var check = 0;
   var perm = Array(n);
   var perm1 = Array(n);
   var count = Array(n);
   var maxPerm = Array(n);
   var maxFlipsCount = 0;
   var m = n - 1;

   for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm1[i] = i;
   var r = n;

   while (true) {
      // write-out the first 30 permutations
      if (check < 30){
         var s = "";
         for(var i=0; i<n; i++) s += (perm1[i]+1).toString();
         check++;
      }

      while (r != 1) { count[r - 1] = r; r--; }
      if (!(perm1[0] == 0 || perm1[m] == m)) {
         for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm[i] = perm1[i];

         var flipsCount = 0;
         var k;

         while (!((k = perm[0]) == 0)) {
            var k2 = (k + 1) >> 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
               var temp = perm[i]; perm[i] = perm[k - i]; perm[k - i] = temp;
            }
            flipsCount++;
         }

         if (flipsCount > maxFlipsCount) {
            maxFlipsCount = flipsCount;
            for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) maxPerm[i] = perm1[i];
         }
      }

      while (true) {
         if (r == n) return maxFlipsCount;
         var perm0 = perm1[0];
         var i = 0;
         while (i < r) {
            var j = i + 1;
            perm1[i] = perm1[j];
            i = j;
         }
         perm1[r] = perm0;

         count[r] = count[r] - 1;
         if (count[r] > 0) break;
         r++;
      }
   }
}

var n = 8;
var ret = fannkuch(n);

var expected = 22;
if (ret != expected)
    throw "ERROR: bad result: expected " + expected + " but got " + ret;

(n) {
   var check = 0;
   var perm = Array(n);
   var perm1 = Array(n);
   var count = Array(n);
   var maxPerm = Array(n);
   var maxFlipsCount = 0;
   var m = n - 1;

   for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm1[i] = i;
   var r = n;

   while (true) {
      // write-out the first 30 permutations
      if (check < 30){
         var s = "";
         for(var i=0; i<n; i++) s += (perm1[i]+1).toString();
         check++;
      }

      while (r != 1) { count[r - 1] = r; r--; }
      if (!(perm1[0] == 0 || perm1[m] == m)) {
         for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm[i] = perm1[i];

         var flipsCount = 0;
         var k;

         while (!((k = perm[0]) == 0)) {
            var k2 = (k + 1) >> 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
               var temp = perm[i]; perm[i] = perm[k - i]; perm[k - i] = temp;
            }
            flipsCount++;
         }

         if (flipsCount > maxFlipsCount) {
            maxFlipsCount = flipsCount;
            for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) maxPerm[i] = perm1[i];
         }
      }

      while (true) {
         if (r == n) return maxFlipsCount;
         var perm0 = perm1[0];
         var i = 0;
         while (i < r) {
            var j = i + 1;
            perm1[i] = perm1[j];
            i = j;
         }
         perm1[r] = perm0;

         count[r] = count[r] - 1;
         if (count[r] > 0) break;
         r++;
      }
   }
}

(w){
var u=this;
if(!(typeof(this)==='number')){
if(!(%_ClassOf(this)==='Number')){
throw MakeTypeError(58,'Number.prototype.toString');
}
u=%_ValueOf(this);
}
if((w===(void 0))||w===10){
return %_NumberToString(u);
}
w=(%_IsSmi(%IS_VAR(w))?w:%NumberToInteger(q(w)));
if(w<2||w>36)throw MakeRangeError(152);
return %NumberToRadixString(u,w);
}

--- Raw source ---
(n) {
   var check = 0;
   var perm = Array(n);
   var perm1 = Array(n);
   var count = Array(n);
   var maxPerm = Array(n);
   var maxFlipsCount = 0;
   var m = n - 1;

   for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm1[i] = i;
   var r = n;

   while (true) {
      // write-out the first 30 permutations
      if (check < 30){
         var s = "";
         for(var i=0; i<n; i++) s += (perm1[i]+1).toString();
         check++;
      }

      while (r != 1) { count[r - 1] = r; r--; }
      if (!(perm1[0] == 0 || perm1[m] == m)) {
         for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm[i] = perm1[i];

         var flipsCount = 0;
         var k;

         while (!((k = perm[0]) == 0)) {
            var k2 = (k + 1) >> 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
               var temp = perm[i]; perm[i] = perm[k - i]; perm[k - i] = temp;
            }
            flipsCount++;
         }

         if (flipsCount > maxFlipsCount) {
            maxFlipsCount = flipsCount;
            for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) maxPerm[i] = perm1[i];
         }
      }

      while (true) {
         if (r == n) return maxFlipsCount;
         var perm0 = perm1[0];
         var i = 0;
         while (i < r) {
            var j = i + 1;
            perm1[i] = perm1[j];
            i = j;
         }
         perm1[r] = perm0;

         count[r] = count[r] - 1;
         if (count[r] > 0) break;
         r++;
      }
   }
}

--- Raw source ---
(n) {
   var check = 0;
   var perm = Array(n);
   var perm1 = Array(n);
   var count = Array(n);
   var maxPerm = Array(n);
   var maxFlipsCount = 0;
   var m = n - 1;

   for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm1[i] = i;
   var r = n;

   while (true) {
      // write-out the first 30 permutations
      if (check < 30){
         var s = "";
         for(var i=0; i<n; i++) s += (perm1[i]+1).toString();
         check++;
      }

      while (r != 1) { count[r - 1] = r; r--; }
      if (!(perm1[0] == 0 || perm1[m] == m)) {
         for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm[i] = perm1[i];

         var flipsCount = 0;
         var k;

         while (!((k = perm[0]) == 0)) {
            var k2 = (k + 1) >> 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
               var temp = perm[i]; perm[i] = perm[k - i]; perm[k - i] = temp;
            }
            flipsCount++;
         }

         if (flipsCount > maxFlipsCount) {
            maxFlipsCount = flipsCount;
            for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) maxPerm[i] = perm1[i];
         }
      }

      while (true) {
         if (r == n) return maxFlipsCount;
         var perm0 = perm1[0];
         var i = 0;
         while (i < r) {
            var j = i + 1;
            perm1[i] = perm1[j];
            i = j;
         }
         perm1[r] = perm0;

         count[r] = count[r] - 1;
         if (count[r] > 0) break;
         r++;
      }
   }
}

--- Raw source ---
(n) {
   var check = 0;
   var perm = Array(n);
   var perm1 = Array(n);
   var count = Array(n);
   var maxPerm = Array(n);
   var maxFlipsCount = 0;
   var m = n - 1;

   for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm1[i] = i;
   var r = n;

   while (true) {
      // write-out the first 30 permutations
      if (check < 30){
         var s = "";
         for(var i=0; i<n; i++) s += (perm1[i]+1).toString();
         check++;
      }

      while (r != 1) { count[r - 1] = r; r--; }
      if (!(perm1[0] == 0 || perm1[m] == m)) {
         for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) perm[i] = perm1[i];

         var flipsCount = 0;
         var k;

         while (!((k = perm[0]) == 0)) {
            var k2 = (k + 1) >> 1;
            for (var i = 0; i < k2; i++) {
               var temp = perm[i]; perm[i] = perm[k - i]; perm[k - i] = temp;
            }
            flipsCount++;
         }

         if (flipsCount > maxFlipsCount) {
            maxFlipsCount = flipsCount;
            for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) maxPerm[i] = perm1[i];
         }
      }

      while (true) {
         if (r == n) return maxFlipsCount;
         var perm0 = perm1[0];
         var i = 0;
         while (i < r) {
            var j = i + 1;
            perm1[i] = perm1[j];
            i = j;
         }
         perm1[r] = perm0;

         count[r] = count[r] - 1;
         if (count[r] > 0) break;
         r++;
      }
   }
}
